				var file     = ["https:\/\/statchasers.com\/wp-content\/et-cache\/1139\/et-divi-dynamic-tb-268-tb-269-1139-late.css"];
				var handle   = document.getElementById('divi-style-inline-inline-css');

			var c = document.body.className;
			c = c.replace(/woocommerce-no-js/, 'woocommerce-js');
			document.body.className = c;
		})();</script>  <script type="application/javascript">//
(function(){
  // ====== CONFIG ======
  var PUBLISH_BASE = 'https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/e/2PACX-1vRrLF5aA8balBffjjRDjNqDk50HltZVZrPlKbFlO_tAFFb-A--6E-ITupGwwYxpplkieWFu0wSjHqpy';
  var EXPECTED = ['RB','WR','QB','TE'];
  var HEAD = { rank:'rank', player:'player', team:'team', pos:'pos', tier:'tier', trend:'trend', note:'note' };

  // localStorage keys
  var LS_HASH = 'SC_ROS_HASH';
  var LS_LAST = 'SC_ROS_LASTTS';

  // ====== UTILS ======
  function ready(fn){ if(document.readyState!=='loading') fn(); else document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', fn); }
  function esc(s){ return String(s==null?'':s).replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;'); }

  // Tiny, fast string hash (djb2)
  function hashString(str){
    var h=5381, i=str.length;
    while(i){ h=((h<<5)+h) ^ str.charCodeAt(--i); }
    // force to unsigned 32-bit and return hex
    return (h>>>0).toString(16);
  }

  function fetchText(url){
    return fetch(url, {mode:'cors', cache:'no-store'}).then(function(r){
      if(!r.ok) throw new Error('HTTP '+r.status);
      return r.text();
    });
  }

  // CSV parser
  function csvParse(t){
    var rows=[],i=0,f='',row=[],q=false,c;
    while(i<t.length){ c=t[i];
      if(q){ if(c=='"'){ if(t[i+1]=='"'){f+='"';i++;} else q=false; } else f+=c; }
      else { if(c=='"') q=true;
             else if(c==','){ row.push(f); f=''; }
             else if(c=='\r'){ }
             else if(c=='\n'){ row.push(f); rows.push(row); row=[]; f=''; }
             else { f+=c; } }
      i++;
    }
    if(f.length||row.length){ row.push(f); rows.push(row); }
    return rows;
  }

  // Strict row builder (filters ghost rows)
  function parseRows(rows){
    if(!rows || !rows.length) return [];
    var headers = rows[0].map(function(h){ return String(h||'').trim(); });
    var out = [];
    for(var r=1;r<rows.length;r++){
      var arr = rows[r]; if(!arr) continue;
      var o = {};
      for(var i=0;i<headers.length;i++){
        var key = (HEAD[headers[i].toLowerCase()] || headers[i].toLowerCase());
        o[key] = arr[i]==null ? '' : String(arr[i]).trim();
      }
      o.rank  = Number(o.rank) || 0;
      o.tier  = Number(o.tier) || 0;
      o.trend = Number(o.trend) || 0;
      o.pos   = (o.pos || '').toUpperCase();
      o.player= (o.player || '');
      o.team  = (o.team || '').toUpperCase();
      o.note  = (o.note  || '');

      var playerClean = o.player.replace(/\u00A0/g,'').replace(/[-]/g,'').trim();
      if(!playerClean) continue; // drop blanks/ghosts
      out.push(o);
    }
    return out;
  }

  // Map {SheetName -> gid}, plus list of all gids
  function getGids(){
    return fetchText(PUBLISH_BASE+'/pubhtml').then(function(html){
      var nameToGid = {};
      html.replace(/data-gid="(\d+)"[^>]*>([^<]+)/g, function(_,gid,name){
        nameToGid[(name||'').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim()] = gid;
      });
      html.replace(/<a[^>]+href="[^"]*gid=(\d+)[^"]*"[^>]*>([\s\S]*?)<\/a>/g, function(_,gid,inner){
        var name = inner.replace(/<[^>]*>/g,'').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();
        if(name) nameToGid[name]=gid;
      });
      var allGids = [];
      html.replace(/gid=(\d+)/g, function(_,gid){ if(allGids.indexOf(gid)<0) allGids.push(gid); });
      return { nameToGid:nameToGid, allGids:allGids };
    });
  }

  // Fetch a tab as CSV text, return both raw text and parsed rows
  function fetchCsvByGid(gid){
    var url = PUBLISH_BASE + '/pub?output=csv&gid=' + encodeURIComponent(gid);
    return fetchText(url).then(function(txt){
      return { raw: txt, data: parseRows(csvParse(txt)) };
    });
  }

  // ====== RENDERING ======
  function initTable(rosData){
    var table = document.getElementById('rosTable'); if(!table) return;
    var tbody = table.querySelector('tbody');
    var search = document.getElementById('rosSearch');
    var tabs   = document.querySelectorAll('.sc-tab');
    var sortKey='rank', sortDir='asc', active='RB', current=[];

    function updateSortIndicators(){
      table.querySelectorAll('thead th').forEach(function(th){ th.removeAttribute('aria-sort'); th.classList.remove('is-sorted'); });
      var th = table.querySelector('thead th[data-key="'+sortKey+'"]');
      if(th){ th.setAttribute('aria-sort', sortDir==='asc'?'ascending':'descending'); th.classList.add('is-sorted'); }
    }

    function render(){
      var data = (rosData[active]||[]).slice();
      var q = (search && search.value || '').toLowerCase().trim();
      var filtered = q ? data.filter(function(r){
        return (r.player||'').toLowerCase().indexOf(q)>-1 ||
               (r.team||'').toLowerCase().indexOf(q)>-1 ||
               (r.pos||'').toLowerCase().indexOf(q)>-1;
      }) : data;

      filtered.sort(function(a,b){
        var cmp=0;
        if(['rank','tier','trend'].indexOf(sortKey)>-1){ cmp=(a[sortKey]||0)-(b[sortKey]||0); }
        else { cmp=String(a[sortKey]).localeCompare(String(b[sortKey])); }
        return sortDir==='asc' ? cmp : -cmp;
      });

      tbody.innerHTML = filtered.map(function(r){
        var cls = r.trend>0?'up':(r.trend<0?'down':'');
        var icon = r.trend>0?'':(r.trend<0?'':'');
        return '<tr>'
          + '<td>'+esc(r.rank)+'</td>'
          + '<td><strong>'+esc(r.player)+'</strong></td>'
          + '<td><span class="sc-badge">'+esc(r.team)+'</span></td>'
          + '<td>'+esc(r.pos||active)+'</td>'
          + '<td><span class="sc-tier">T'+esc(r.tier||'')+'</span></td>'
          + '<td><span class="sc-trend '+cls+'">'+icon+' '+(r.trend===0?'0':Math.abs(r.trend||0))+'</span></td>'
          + '<td><span class="sc-note">'+esc(r.note||'')+'</span></td>'
        + '</tr>';
      }).join('');

      current = filtered;
      updateSortIndicators();
      // DO NOT touch the timestamp here
      window.SC_ROS = { reload: loadAll, getVisible: function(){ return current.slice(); } };
    }

    tabs.forEach(function(btn){
      btn.addEventListener('click', function(){
        tabs.forEach(function(b){ b.classList.remove('is-active'); b.setAttribute('aria-selected','false'); });
        btn.classList.add('is-active'); btn.setAttribute('aria-selected','true');
        active = btn.dataset.pos; sortKey='rank'; sortDir='asc'; render();
      });
    });
    table.querySelectorAll('thead th').forEach(function(th){
      th.addEventListener('click', function(){
        var key = th.getAttribute('data-key'); if(!key) return;
        if(sortKey===key) sortDir = (sortDir==='asc'?'desc':'asc'); else { sortKey=key; sortDir='asc'; }
        render();
      });
    });
    search && search.addEventListener('input', render);

    render();
  }

  // ====== LOAD FLOW (with content hash for timestamp) ======
  function loadAll(){
    var host = document.getElementById('ros'); if(!host) return;
    var updatedEl = document.getElementById('rosUpdatedBottom');

    getGids().then(function(info){
      var nameToGid = info.nameToGid || {};
      var allGids   = info.allGids || [];
      var want = {};
      EXPECTED.forEach(function(n){
        if(nameToGid[n]) { want[n]=nameToGid[n]; return; }
        var k = Object.keys(nameToGid).find(function(x){ return x.toLowerCase().trim()===n.toLowerCase(); });
        if(k) want[n]=nameToGid[k];
      });

      var jobs = EXPECTED.map(function(n){
        if(!want[n]) return Promise.resolve({ raw:'', data:[] });
        return fetchCsvByGid(want[n]).catch(function(){ return { raw:'', data:[] }; });
      });

      // If some tabs are unmapped, sniff remaining gids and infer by Pos majority
      var missing = EXPECTED.filter(function(n){ return !want[n]; });
      var sniffPromise = Promise.resolve([]);
      if(missing.length){
        var pool = allGids.filter(function(g){ return Object.values(want).indexOf(g)<0; });
        sniffPromise = Promise.all(pool.map(function(g){
          return fetchCsvByGid(g).then(function(res){ return [g,res]; }).catch(function(){ return [g,{raw:'',data:[]}]; });
        })).then(function(pairs){
          pairs.forEach(function(pair){
            var gid=pair[0], res=pair[1], data=res.data||[];
            if(!data.length) return;
            var counts={RB:0,WR:0,QB:0,TE:0};
            for(var i=0;i<data.length;i++){
              var p=(data[i].pos||'').toUpperCase();
              if(counts.hasOwnProperty(p)) counts[p]++;
            }
            var best=Object.keys(counts).sort(function(a,b){ return counts[b]-counts[a]; })[0];
            if(counts[best]>0 && !want[best]) want[best]=gid;
          });
          var extraJobs = missing.map(function(n){
            if(!want[n]) return Promise.resolve({raw:'',data:[]});
            return fetchCsvByGid(want[n]).catch(function(){ return {raw:'',data:[]}; });
          });
          return Promise.all(extraJobs);
        });
      }

      return Promise.all(jobs).then(function(primary){
        return sniffPromise.then(function(extra){
          var results = primary.slice();
          if(extra && extra.length){
            var idxByName = {RB:0,WR:1,QB:2,TE:3};
            missing.forEach(function(n,i){ results[idxByName[n]] = extra[i]; });
          }

          // Build combined text hash (stable order RB,WR,QB,TE)
          var combinedRaw = results.map(function(r){ return r.raw||''; }).join('\n---TAB---\n');
          var newHash = hashString(combinedRaw);

          // Decide last-updated value based on hash vs localStorage
          var storedHash = null, storedTime = null;
          try {
            storedHash = localStorage.getItem(LS_HASH);
            storedTime = localStorage.getItem(LS_LAST);
          } catch(e) {}

          var displayTime;
          if(storedHash && storedHash === newHash && storedTime){
            // No change -> keep prior timestamp
            displayTime = storedTime;
          } else {
            // Content changed (or first load) -> set to now and store
            displayTime = new Date().toLocaleString();
            try {
              localStorage.setItem(LS_HASH, newHash);
              localStorage.setItem(LS_LAST, displayTime);
            } catch(e) {}
          }
          if(updatedEl) updatedEl.textContent = displayTime;

          // Build rosData for rendering
          var rosData = {RB:[],WR:[],QB:[],TE:[]};
          EXPECTED.forEach(function(name, idx){
            rosData[name] = (results[idx] && results[idx].data) ? results[idx].data : [];
            (rosData[name]||[]).forEach(function(r){ if(!r.pos) r.pos=name; });
          });

          initTable(rosData);
        });
      });
    }).catch(function(e){
      console.error('ROS load error', e);
      var updatedEl = document.getElementById('rosUpdatedBottom');
      if(updatedEl) updatedEl.textContent = 'error loading data';
    });
  }

  ready(loadAll);
})();
//</script> <script>document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {

  function getMenu() {
    return document.querySelector(".et_mobile_menu");
  }

  function collapseAll(menu) {
    if (!menu) return;
    menu.querySelectorAll(".menu-item-has-children.visible").forEach(li => li.classList.remove("visible"));
  }

  // Collapse on load
  collapseAll(getMenu());

  // Collapse every time hamburger opens (Divi re-renders menu)
  const hamburger = document.querySelector(".mobile_nav .mobile_menu_bar");
  if (hamburger) {
    hamburger.addEventListener("click", function () {
      setTimeout(() => collapseAll(getMenu()), 50);
    });
  }

  //  Event delegation: works even after Divi rebuilds the menu
  document.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
    const menu = getMenu();
    if (!menu) return;

    // Clicked a parent link OR Divi's dropdown arrow
    const parentLink = e.target.closest(".et_mobile_menu .menu-item-has-children > a");
    const arrow = e.target.closest(".et_mobile_menu .menu-item-has-children > .et_mobile_arrow");

    if (!parentLink && !arrow) return;

    const li = (parentLink || arrow).closest(".menu-item-has-children");
    if (!li || !menu.contains(li)) return;

    // Prevent navigation on parent click (we want expand/collapse)
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();

    // True accordion: close siblings
    const siblings = li.parentElement ? li.parentElement.querySelectorAll(":scope > .menu-item-has-children.visible") : [];
    siblings.forEach(openLi => { if (openLi !== li) openLi.classList.remove("visible"); });

    // Toggle this section
    li.classList.toggle("visible");
  }, true);

  window.addEventListener("scroll", revealOnScroll);

//# sourceURL=et-builder-modules-script-sticky-js-extra</script> <script type="text/javascript">(function() {
